# Description_Notes_and_Keywords
#   Description: The purpose of this collection was to characterize 
# # stand-level tree growth patterns for comparison with 
# # satellite-derived vegetation indices. 
# # 
# # Terrain was flat and tree cover at the site was quite sparse 
# # (10s of trees/ha). Understory of dwarf alnus, betula, salix, 
# # and ledum spp. Locally, this species is referred to as 
# # Larix cajanderi Mayr.  The ITRDB uses the synonym 
# # Larix gmelinii (Rupr.) Kuzen.   NOAA Template Raw Measurements file added 2019-04-08.
